<script>
        // Micro-interaction for log expanding
        document.querySelectorAll('.group').forEach(item => {
            item.addEventListener('click', function() {
                this.classList.toggle('bg-surface-container-highest/20');
            });
        });

        // Atmospheric effect: periodic system log generation
        const terminal = document.querySelector('.terminal-scroll');
        const eventTypes = ['INFO', 'WARN', 'SYNC', 'POST'];
        const colors = ['text-tertiary', 'text-secondary-fixed-dim', 'text-primary', 'text-on-tertiary-container'];
        
        setInterval(() => {
            if(terminal.children.length > 50) return; // Prevent infinite bloat
            
            const now = new Date();
            const time = `${now.getHours()}:${now.getMinutes()}:${now.getSeconds()}.${now.getMilliseconds().toString().slice(0,2)}`;
            const typeIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * eventTypes.length);
            
            const div = document.createElement('div');
            div.className = 'group border-b border-outline-variant/5 py-sm hover:bg-surface-container/30 transition-colors cursor-pointer opacity-0 transition-opacity duration-500';
            div.innerHTML = `
                <div class="flex gap-md">
                    <span class="text-outline-variant shrink-0">${time}</span>
                    <span class="${colors[typeIndex]} shrink-0 font-bold">[${eventTypes[typeIndex]}]</span>
                    <span class="text-on-surface-variant">Incoming packet from external node node_x${Math.floor(Math.random()*999)} - verification successful.</span>
                </div>
            `;
            
            terminal.insertBefore(div, terminal.lastElementChild);
            setTimeout(() => div.classList.remove('opacity-0'), 10);
            
            // Auto-scroll if near bottom
            if(terminal.scrollTop + terminal.clientHeight > terminal.scrollHeight - 100) {
                terminal.scrollTop = terminal.scrollHeight;
            }
        }, 4000);
    </script>
</body></html>

<script>
        // Micro-interaction: Drag & Drop Zone Glow Effect
        const dropZone = document.querySelector('.border-dashed');
        if (dropZone) {
            dropZone.addEventListener('dragover', (e) => {
                e.preventDefault();
                dropZone.classList.add('border-tertiary', 'bg-tertiary/5');
            });
            dropZone.addEventListener('dragleave', () => {
                dropZone.classList.remove('border-tertiary', 'bg-tertiary/5');
            });
        }

        // Simulating some dynamic progress movement
        setInterval(() => {
            const bars = document.querySelectorAll('.animate-pulse');
            bars.forEach(bar => {
                const parent = bar.parentElement;
                if (parent) {
                    const currentWidth = parseFloat(parent.style.width || "92");
                    if (currentWidth < 100) {
                        const newWidth = Math.min(100, currentWidth + 0.1);
                        parent.style.width = newWidth + '%';
                        const text = parent.closest('.space-y-xs').querySelector('.flex span:last-child');
                        if (text) text.innerText = Math.floor(newWidth) + '%';
                    }
                }
            });
        }, 1000);
    </script>

<script>
        // Micro-interactions for keyboard shortcuts simulation
        document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
            if (e.key === 'Escape') {
                const rejectBtn = document.querySelector('button.bg-error');
                rejectBtn.classList.add('scale-95', 'opacity-50');
                setTimeout(() => rejectBtn.classList.remove('scale-95', 'opacity-50'), 150);
                console.log('Rejecting workflow...');
            }
            if (e.key === 'Enter' && (e.metaKey || e.ctrlKey)) {
                const approveBtn = document.querySelector('button.bg-tertiary');
                approveBtn.classList.add('scale-95', 'opacity-50');
                setTimeout(() => approveBtn.classList.remove('scale-95', 'opacity-50'), 150);
                console.log('Approving workflow...');
            }
        });

        // Toggle list items active state
        const listItems = document.querySelectorAll('section:first-of-type .p-md');
        listItems.forEach(item => {
            item.addEventListener('click', () => {
                listItems.forEach(i => {
                    i.classList.remove('cyber-border-active', 'glow-cyan', 'glass-panel');
                    i.classList.add('border', 'border-outline-variant/20', 'bg-surface-container-lowest');
                });
                item.classList.remove('border', 'border-outline-variant/20', 'bg-surface-container-lowest');
                item.classList.add('cyber-border-active', 'glow-cyan', 'glass-panel');
            });
        });
    </script>

                    setInterval(() => {
                        const div = document.createElement('div');
                        div.innerText = logs[i % logs.length];
                        const container = document.getElementById('log-stream');
                        container.appendChild(div);
                        if (container.children.length > 15) container.removeChild(container.firstChild);
                        i++;
                    }, 2000);
                </script>

        // Micro-interaction: Randomize heatmap opacity slightly for 'real-time' effect
        setInterval(() => {
            const cells = document.querySelectorAll('.grid-cols-20 div');
            const randomIdx = Math.floor(Math.random() * cells.length);
            const originalOpacity = cells[randomIdx].style.opacity || "0.5";
            cells[randomIdx].style.transition = "opacity 1s ease";
            cells[randomIdx].style.opacity = Math.random();
            setTimeout(() => cells[randomIdx].style.opacity = originalOpacity, 1000);
        }, 100);
    </script>

<script>
        // Micro-interactions and atmospheric effects
        document.querySelectorAll('.glass-panel').forEach(card => {
            card.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => {
                const rect = card.getBoundingClientRect();
                const x = e.clientX - rect.left;
                const y = e.clientY - rect.top;
                card.style.setProperty('--mouse-x', `${x}px`);
                card.style.setProperty('--mouse-y', `${y}px`);
                
                // Add a subtle spotlight effect
                card.style.background = `radial-gradient(600px circle at ${x}px ${y}px, rgba(47, 217, 244, 0.03), transparent 40%), rgba(10, 12, 16, 0.7)`;
            });
            
            card.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => {
                card.style.background = 'rgba(10, 12, 16, 0.7)';
            });
        });

        // Pulsing active state simulation
        const bars = document.querySelectorAll('.h-8 .flex-1');
        setInterval(() => {
            bars.forEach(bar => {
                const height = Math.floor(Math.random() * 80) + 20;
                bar.style.height = height + '%';
            });
        }, 1200);
    </script>

<script>
        // Atmospheric parallax on hero image
        window.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => {
            const heroImg = document.querySelector('img[data-alt*="futuristic data center"]');
            if (heroImg) {
                const moveX = (e.clientX - window.innerWidth / 2) * 0.01;
                const moveY = (e.clientY - window.innerHeight / 2) * 0.01;
                heroImg.style.transform = `scale(1.1) translate(${moveX}px, ${moveY}px)`;
            }
        });

        // Search bar interaction
        const searchInput = document.querySelector('input[placeholder="Search assets..."]');
        searchInput.addEventListener('focus', () => {
            searchInput.parentElement.classList.add('border-tertiary');
            searchInput.parentElement.classList.add('bg-tertiary/5');
        });
        searchInput.addEventListener('blur', () => {
            searchInput.parentElement.classList.remove('border-tertiary');
            searchInput.parentElement.classList.remove('bg-tertiary/5');
        });
    </script>

        // Micro-interaction for hover glow on glass panels
        document.querySelectorAll('.glass-panel').forEach(card => {
            card.addEventListener('mousemove', e => {
                const rect = card.getBoundingClientRect();
                const x = e.clientX - rect.left;
                const y = e.clientY - rect.top;
                card.style.setProperty('--mouse-x', `${x}px`);
                card.style.setProperty('--mouse-y', `${y}px`);
            });
        });
    </script>

<script>
        // Micro-interactions for the "interactive" feel
        document.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => {
            const canvas = document.getElementById('memory-canvas');
            const x = e.clientX / window.innerWidth;
            const y = e.clientY / window.innerHeight;
            
            canvas.style.background = `radial-gradient(circle at ${x * 100}% ${y * 100}%, #0b1c30 0%, #031427 100%)`;
        });

        // Search highlight interaction
        const searchInput = document.querySelector('input');
        searchInput.addEventListener('focus', () => {
            searchInput.parentElement.classList.add('scale-[1.01]');
        });
        searchInput.addEventListener('blur', () => {
            searchInput.parentElement.classList.remove('scale-[1.01]');
        });
    </script>

<script>
        // Micro-interactions for input focus
        const inputs = document.querySelectorAll('input');
        inputs.forEach(input => {
            input.addEventListener('focus', () => {
                input.parentElement.classList.add('border-tertiary');
            });
            input.addEventListener('blur', () => {
                input.parentElement.classList.remove('border-tertiary');
            });
        });

        // Toggle interaction simulation
        const toggles = document.querySelectorAll('.w-10.h-5');
        toggles.forEach(toggle => {
            toggle.addEventListener('click', () => {
                const knob = toggle.querySelector('div');
                const isActive = toggle.classList.contains('bg-tertiary/20');
                
                if(isActive) {
                    toggle.classList.remove('bg-tertiary/20', 'border-tertiary/50');
                    toggle.classList.add('bg-surface-variant', 'border-outline-variant');
                    knob.classList.remove('right-0.5', 'bg-tertiary', 'shadow-tertiary/50');
                    knob.classList.add('left-0.5', 'bg-outline');
                } else {
                    toggle.classList.add('bg-tertiary/20', 'border-tertiary/50');
                    toggle.classList.remove('bg-surface-variant', 'border-outline-variant');
                    knob.classList.add('right-0.5', 'bg-tertiary', 'shadow-tertiary/50');
                    knob.classList.remove('left-0.5', 'bg-outline');
                }
            });
        });
    </script>

<script>
        // Micro-interaction for cards
        document.querySelectorAll('.glass-card').forEach(card => {
            card.addEventListener('mousedown', () => {
                card.style.transform = 'scale(0.98)';
                card.style.opacity = '0.9';
            });
            card.addEventListener('mouseup', () => {
                card.style.transform = 'scale(1)';
                card.style.opacity = '1';
            });
        });

        // Search bar focus effect
        const searchInput = document.querySelector('input[type="text"]');
        searchInput.addEventListener('focus', () => {
            searchInput.parentElement.classList.add('ring-1', 'ring-tertiary');
        });
        searchInput.addEventListener('blur', () => {
            searchInput.parentElement.classList.remove('ring-1', 'ring-tertiary');
        });
    </script>

        // Simple scroll reveal interaction
        window.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
            const elements = document.querySelectorAll('.glass-panel');
            elements.forEach(el => {
                const rect = el.getBoundingClientRect();
                const isVisible = rect.top < window.innerHeight - 100;
                if (isVisible) {
                    el.style.opacity = '1';
                    el.style.transform = 'translateY(0)';
                }
            });
        });

        // Initialize state for elements that should animate on scroll
        document.querySelectorAll('.glass-panel').forEach(el => {
            el.style.opacity = '0.8';
            el.style.transition = 'all 0.6s cubic-bezier(0.22, 1, 0.36, 1)';
        });
    </script>

<h2 class="font-headline-lg text-headline-lg text-on-surface mb-lg text-center">Billing Intelligence</h2>
<div class="space-y-md">

<div class="flex justify-between items-center">
<span class="font-label-sm text-on-surface text-body-md">How are credits calculated?</span>
<span class="material-symbols-outlined text-tertiary transition-transform">expand_more</span>
</div>
<div class="faq-content h-0 overflow-hidden opacity-0 transition-all">
<p class="pt-md text-on-surface-variant font-body-md">Credits are consumed based on the token usage of LLMs, vector database read/write operations, and swarm orchestration time. Each action has a transparent unit price visible in your Studio dashboard.</p>

<div class="flex justify-between items-center">

<span class="material-symbols-outlined text-tertiary transition-transform">expand_more</span>
</div>
<div class="faq-content h-0 overflow-hidden opacity-0 transition-all">
<p class="pt-md text-on-surface-variant font-body-md">Builder and Company plans allow for a 30-day rollover period for up to 20% of your monthly credit allowance. Enterprise plans feature custom rollover terms.</p>
</div>

</div>
<div class="faq-content h-0 overflow-hidden opacity-0 transition-all">
<p class="pt-md text-on-surface-variant font-body-md">We automatically notify you when you reach 80% and 100% of your usage. You can enable "Auto-Topup" or your workflows will pause to prevent unexpected overage charges.</p>

<script>
        // FAQ Accordion Logic
        function toggleFaq(el) {
            const content = el.querySelector('.faq-content');
            const icon = el.querySelector('.material-symbols-outlined');
            const isOpen = !content.classList.contains('h-0');

            // Close all first (optional)
            document.querySelectorAll('.faq-content').forEach(c => {
                c.classList.add('h-0', 'opacity-0');
                c.previousElementSibling.querySelector('.material-symbols-outlined').style.transform = 'rotate(0deg)';
            });

            if (!isOpen) {
                content.classList.remove('h-0', 'opacity-0');
                content.classList.add('h-auto', 'opacity-100');
                icon.style.transform = 'rotate(180deg)';
            }
        }

        // Billing Toggle Logic
        const toggle = document.getElementById('billing-toggle');
        const thumb = document.getElementById('toggle-thumb');
        let isYearly = false;

        toggle.addEventListener('click', () => {
            isYearly = !isYearly;
            thumb.style.transform = isYearly ? 'translateX(24px)' : 'translateX(0)';
            
            // Visual feedback for pricing change
            document.querySelectorAll('.font-display-lg').forEach(price => {
                if (price.innerText.includes('$')) {
                    const baseVal = parseInt(price.innerText.replace('$', ''));
                    if (isYearly) {
                        price.innerText = `$${Math.round(baseVal * 0.8)}`;
                    } else {
                        // Simplified reverse for demo
                        price.innerText = `$${Math.round(baseVal / 0.8)}`;
                    }
                }
            });
        });

        // Atmospheric mouse effect (subtle)
        document.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => {
            const x = (e.clientX / window.innerWidth) * 100;
            const y = (e.clientY / window.innerHeight) * 100;
            document.body.style.backgroundImage = `radial-gradient(circle at ${x}% ${y}%, rgba(47, 217, 244, 0.03) 0%, transparent 40%)`;
        });
    </script>
</body></html>

<!-- FAB (Suppressed on this deep dashboard view per rules, but included if needed for specific logic) -->
<script>
        // Micro-interaction: Node Pulse Effect
        document.querySelectorAll('.group\\/node').forEach(node => {
            node.addEventListener('mouseenter', () => {
                node.querySelector('.glass-panel').style.transform = 'scale(1.05) translateY(-5px)';
                node.querySelector('.glass-panel').style.boxShadow = '0 0 25px -5px rgba(47, 217, 244, 0.4)';
            });
            node.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => {
                node.querySelector('.glass-panel').style.transform = 'scale(1) translateY(0)';
                node.querySelector('.glass-panel').style.boxShadow = 'none';
            });
        });

        // Simulating Real-time Delegation Log Updates
        const logElement = document.querySelector('.custom-scrollbar');
        const prefixes = ['[14:02:28]', '[14:02:31]', '[14:02:35]', '[14:02:39]'];
        const messages = [
            'NODE_GAMMA -> Storage: Commit "Task_State_Final"',
            'ORCHESTRATOR: Balancing cluster "US-EAST-01"',
            'Safety: Policy check passed for Swarm_Exec_77',
            'Telemetry: All agents reporting optimal status'
        ];
        let index = 0;

        setInterval(() => {
            if (index < messages.length) {
                const newLog = document.createElement('div');
                newLog.className = 'p-sm bg-surface-container-low/50 rounded border-l-2 border-outline-variant animate-pulse';
                newLog.innerHTML = `<span class="text-on-surface-variant">${prefixes[index]}</span> ${messages[index]}`;
                logElement.appendChild(newLog);
                logElement.scrollTop = logElement.scrollHeight;
                index++;
            }
        }, 4000);
    </script>
